To make future work easier, you can use piping to send the output of the command directly to another command (including hq) without typing it in again.
To send the line count of the customer datavase straight to hq, use this command:
cat ./customer_db.txt | wc -l | hq
cat will normally just print the file, but using |, you can redirect that to the line-count program.  Using one last pipe, we redirect the output of the line counter to hq
